\maketitle

Research Question:
\textit{How (and why) has the rate of walks changed over the history of baseball?}

Which Datafile from the Lahman package would you use to answer this
question?

\vspace{1in}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\KeywordTok{library}\NormalTok{(tidyverse)}
\KeywordTok{library}\NormalTok{(Lahman)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
## Warning: package 'Lahman' was built under R version 3.5.3
\end{verbatim}

\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{Teams}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

On page 35 of the text, there is a list of the five main dplyr verbs
(and group\_by). Below, briefly describe what each does.

\begin{itemize}
\item
  \texttt{select}
\item
  \texttt{filter}
\item
  \texttt{arrange}
\item
  \texttt{mutate}
\item
  \texttt{summarize}
\item
  \texttt{group\_by}
\end{itemize}

Discuss how you could use these verbs and the Teams database to
calculate the walk rate (per nine innings). Write your code below.
\vspace{0.5in}

\newpage

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{#Calculate the walk rate per 9 innings by season}
\NormalTok{Teams }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }
\StringTok{  }\KeywordTok{group_by}\NormalTok{(yearID) }\OperatorTok{%>%}
\StringTok{  }\KeywordTok{summarize}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{walks_per_game =} \KeywordTok{sum}\NormalTok{(BB)}\OperatorTok{/}\KeywordTok{sum}\NormalTok{(G),}
            \DataTypeTok{SO_per_game =} \KeywordTok{sum}\NormalTok{(SO)}\OperatorTok{/}\KeywordTok{sum}\NormalTok{(G)) ->}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{walks}

\NormalTok{walks }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{head}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

What trends do you observe in walks? \vspace{0.75in}

The previous plot tells us nothing about \texttt{why} we observe
changes. Briefly explain two other analyses we might conduct to better
understand trends in walks. Identify the appropriate Datafiles for these
analyses. \vspace{0.75in}

Let's see if the ratio of walks to strikeouts tells us anything
interesting. Without looking on the next page, write the code you would
use to calculate the ratio of walks to strikeouts by season.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{walks =}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{walks }\OperatorTok{%>%}
\StringTok{  }\KeywordTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{walks_SO_ratio =}\NormalTok{ walks_per_game}\OperatorTok{/}\NormalTok{SO_per_game)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}
